you type out a “WHY DIDN’T YOU TAKE THE OFFER TO GET PAID EARLY” comment, let me be clear… I am grateful that after years of hard work, I attract clients who give a eff about their freelancers. But I \n<strong>prepared my business for moments like this.</strong> Did I predict that a pandemic would single-handedly \n<a href=\"https://www.bbc.com/news/business-51706225\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">destroy the world economy</a>&nbsp;in a few weeks? Not necessarily. But thanks to a decade of \n<a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/sophiakle/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">work as a disaster policy researcher and emergency manager</a>, I know there’s a way to \n<strong>plan for a recession, pandemic or anything else that could put you out of business</strong>. So I made the most of my \n<a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/coronavirus/2019-ncov/prevent-getting-sick/social-distancing.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">social distancing time</a>&nbsp;and broke it down for you – step by step. By the time you finish this article, you’ll learn… \n<ul> \n <li>Why government officials don’t know a thing about running a business (let alone preparing them)</li> \n <li>What the world’s greatest copywriting formula can teach you about emergency planning</li> \n <li>The 5 types of emergency scenarios your business should be thinking about</li> \n</ul> So turn off Netflix, grab a cup of coffee or tea, and let’s get started. \n<!-- /wp:html --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":1} --> \n<h1 id=\"h.1hizr4gh4py8\">Why government officials don’t know a thing about running a business (let alone preparing them)</h1> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Here’s the truth: \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<strong>Most</strong> government workers advising businesses on emergency planning don’t have a clue what it means to run a business. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> And when I say “most”, I mean me. Back then, at least. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Why would I? I had a 50 hour work week, $0 deductible health insurance (Good luck finding that as a freelancer), and a pension plan. So when I gave up my cushy government job to become a freelance copywriter, I found myself imagining all the things that could go wrong with my new career. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Like what happens if I have no clients for months on end? \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> What if I lose our Internet connection right before an important presentation? \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Or what if I (gulp) expose myself to a killer virus with no known cure? \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> So I went back to my own experience as an emergency manager. What exactly did I tell business owners when they asked for advice on how to get prepared? \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> First, I would have scheduled an hour-long presentation and showed \n<a href=\"https://www.fema.gov/media-library/assets/videos/152704\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">a video similar to this</a>… \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<video poster=\"//www.fema.gov/media-library-data/1510948144061-5aaa5ecf56d68ea5e2d47b3f7f7f5e15/ReadyBusinessSpaceVideo_small.png\" preload=\"metadata\" controls=\"controls\" width=\"462\" height=\"260\"></video> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<a href=\"https://www.fema.gov/media-library/assets/videos/152704\">View in FEMA Multimedia Library</a> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Then I would send them to a \n<a href=\"https://disastersafety.org/business-protection/ofb-ez/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">website with worksheets</a>&nbsp;like the one on Knowing Your Risks below… \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":25079} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img class=\"wp-image-25079\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/FireShot-Capture-013-disastersafety.org_.png?resize=800%2C900&amp;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/FireShot-Capture-013-disastersafety.org_.png?resize=800%2C900&amp;ssl=1 800w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/FireShot-Capture-013-disastersafety.org_.png?resize=267%2C300&amp;ssl=1 267w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/FireShot-Capture-013-disastersafety.org_.png?resize=133%2C150&amp;ssl=1 133w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/FireShot-Capture-013-disastersafety.org_.png?resize=768%2C864&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/FireShot-Capture-013-disastersafety.org_.png?w=807&amp;ssl=1 807w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" />\n </figure> \n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":25078} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img class=\"wp-image-25078\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-25-at-4.13.20-PM.png?ssl=1\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-25-at-4.13.20-PM.png?w=658&amp;ssl=1 658w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-25-at-4.13.20-PM.png?resize=300%2C145&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-25-at-4.13.20-PM.png?resize=150%2C73&amp;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 658px) 100vw, 658px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" />\n </figure> \n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> And assuming that these 2 things didn’t bore the living daylights out of them, I might send over the following \n<a href=\"https://www.ready.gov/business-continuity-plan\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">business continuity planning diagram from Ready.gov</a>.Source: \n<a href=\"https://www.ready.gov/business-continuity-plan\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Ready.gov</a> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Did I do my duty as an emergency manager? Sure. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Did this help business owners protect themselves from an emergency? Probably, but who has the time to do it all? We’re called “small businesses” for a reason. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> So forget I showed you any of that, and let’s talk about what you can do to \n<strong>get your business prepared, using a copywriting formula</strong>&nbsp;you may be familiar with. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":1} --> \n<h1 id=\"h.dls3pvoz6ds7\">What Problem, Agitation, Solution Can Teach You About Emergency Planning</h1> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> If you’ve ever written a single line of copy, you should know that the world’s greatest copywriting formula is Problem, Agitation, Solution (P.A.S.). \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Why does P.A.S. work so well? Because it’s simple, it’s effective, and it takes the \n<a href=\"https://theconversioncopywriter.com/problem-agitation-solution-framework/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">reader seamlessly through the stages of awareness.</a> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> And emergency managers do the same thing to practice their emergency plans. We just call it a \n<strong>tabletop exercise</strong>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> For emergency management newbies (Which is probably 99% of you because you’re reading a copywriting blog), here are 4 phases of running an emergency preparedness program: \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true} --> \n<ol> \n <li>Planning,</li> \n <li>Implementation,</li> \n <li>Testing &amp; Exercise, and</li> \n <li>Program Improvement.</li> \n</ol> \n<!-- /wp:list --> \n<!-- wp:image --> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img alt=\"\" />\n</figure> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":25070} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img class=\"wp-image-25070\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-31-at-11.36.01-AM.png?ssl=1\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-31-at-11.36.01-AM.png?w=496&amp;ssl=1 496w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-31-at-11.36.01-AM.png?resize=300%2C238&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-31-at-11.36.01-AM.png?resize=150%2C119&amp;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 496px) 100vw, 496px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" />\n </figure> \n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<em>Source: Ready.gov</em> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<strong>Planning</strong>&nbsp;is more or less writing all the procedures of what you would do if a disaster happens and putting in a giant 3-ring binder… \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":25089} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img class=\"wp-image-25089\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/new-binder-smell.gif?ssl=1\" alt=\"\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" />\n </figure> \n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<img alt=\"\" />\n<strong>Testing &amp; Exercise</strong>&nbsp;is what happens when the entity (in this case, your business) goes through the mental or physical process of seeing if what you wrote down as a procedure works for a specific scenario. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> So once you \n<strong>Plan</strong>, you \n<strong>Implement</strong>&nbsp;what you wrote down, run through a \n<strong>Test or Exercise</strong>, and then do \n<strong>Program Improvement</strong>&nbsp;as a result of the \n<strong>Test or Exercise</strong>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Anyway, within \n<strong>Testing &amp; Exercises</strong>&nbsp;are various types of drills you can do within an emergency management program, and the one you need to know about is called a \n<strong>tabletop exercise</strong>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> A \n<strong>tabletop exercise</strong>&nbsp;is one of the lowest-touch exercises to pull off because all it takes is a select group of people, a few hours and a conversation centered around a scenario or two. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> It works because you \n<strong>verbally or mentally walk through a Problem, Agitation, and Solution…</strong> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> And you can do it without, errr… physically recreating an emergency… \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":25074} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img class=\"wp-image-25074\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/firedrill.gif?ssl=1\" alt=\"\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" />\n </figure> \n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<img alt=\"\" />Or experiencing a real emergency first-hand. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":25072} --> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img class=\"wp-image-25072\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/twister_.gif?ssl=1\" alt=\"twister \" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" />\n</figure> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Now that you understand what a tabletop exercise is let me walk you through \n<strong>5 emergency scenarios</strong>&nbsp;that could affect your freelance copywriting business. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> The emergency scenarios are: \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true} --> \n<ol> \n <li>You can’t work for an extended period</li> \n <li>The physical place you work is malfunctioning or uninhabitable</li> \n <li>External threats to your business assets</li> \n <li>You are under government order to stay where you are</li> \n <li>You lose work or can’t find work due to economic conditions</li> \n</ol> \n<!-- /wp:list --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> I’ll give you a specific example of each and break it down using the \n<strong>Problem, Agitation, Solution</strong>&nbsp;formula. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading --> \n<h2 id=\"h.a9qcm7woco3b\">ONE: You can’t work for an extended period</h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<em>Something like: A chronic disease diagnosis or a heavy body injury (Like getting into a car accident).</em> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.vlgrk5ytuxqa\">Problem</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> You’re feeling tired and burnt out from serving clients, writing a book, and pursuing a graduate degree. You decide to take some time off to do self-care and schedule that yearly checkup you’ve been putting off for the last 15 years. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> You notice something’s off with your body and let your doctor know, who orders a scan “just to be safe,” but thinks you’re fine. Which you are. Phew. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.sd30ahyzcky\">Agitation</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> 3 months later, you go back in for another scan “just to be safe,” and what was “fine” 3 months ago is a tumor. So you go back for surgery to remove the growth. And then do another 9-hour surgery so tumors don’t come back. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> The surgery went fine, but the doctors also think you might have bladder cancer too. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Oh, did I mention that your dad died in a car wreck a few weeks ago? \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.knmxrrjg5zc2\">Solution</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":25071} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img class=\"wp-image-25071\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/IMG_1380.jpg?resize=800%2C800&amp;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/IMG_1380.jpg?resize=800%2C800&amp;ssl=1 800w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/IMG_1380.jpg?resize=300%2C300&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/IMG_1380.jpg?resize=150%2C150&amp;ssl=1 150w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/IMG_1380.jpg?resize=768%2C768&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/IMG_1380.jpg?resize=400%2C400&amp;ssl=1 400w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/IMG_1380.jpg?resize=350%2C350&amp;ssl=1 350w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/IMG_1380.jpg?resize=720%2C720&amp;ssl=1 720w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/IMG_1380.jpg?w=960&amp;ssl=1 960w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" />\n </figure> \n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Note that this isn’t a B.S. scenario; this was my husband’s life in 2015. He’s been cancer-free since 2016. I won’t bore you with the details of his recovery, but I will leave you with this photo of us before his 9-hour surgery. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Assuming this \n<em>hasn’t</em>&nbsp;happened to you, let me take you through my thought process of planning for the possibility of cancer relapse. Ultimately, it came down to 3 things… \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.9t87xn2sv2wg\">1. Really good health insurance</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> If you’re a \n<a href=\"https://www.raconteur.net/risk-management/insurance-cover-freelancers\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">freelancer, health insurance sucks</a>. It’s even worse when you’re dealing with a chronic disease that requires regular lab work and tests. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> So I focused on changing our business structure to qualify for a group health insurance plan. It’s almost (but not quite) as good as what I had as a full-time employee. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.pefccixph50o\">2. Long-term disability insurance</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> We decided against purchasing \n<a href=\"https://www.policygenius.com/blog/long-term-disability-insurance-for-freelancers-101/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">long-term disability insurance</a>&nbsp;but it’s worth mentioning. Buying a long-term disability policy can give you up to 90 days worth of wages if you can’t work for whatever reason. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.c8338weeh7tv\">3. Life insurance</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> We also decided against this. Life insurance doesn’t make sense if you have a pre-existing health condition, but it’s \n<a href=\"https://blog.freelancersunion.org/2014/12/02/everything-freelancers-need-know-about-life-insurance/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">worth some research</a>&nbsp;if you’re a healthy individual and want to make sure your family is taken care of if something happens to you. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.9li3p9qztij2\">To sum it all up</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Based on my personal experience, preparing for this scenario is all about figuring out how you can cover costs if you can’t earn income for an extended period. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> If buying insurance is difficult or not an option, you could sub all of these things by having an \n<a href=\"https://www.daveramsey.com/blog/quick-guide-to-your-emergency-fund\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">emergency fund</a>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading --> \n<h2 id=\"h.9bfvcqe2nvmi\">TWO: The physical place you conduct your work is malfunctioning or uninhabitable</h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<em>Something like: A power outage, fire, hurricane, tornado, earthquake.</em> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.qjyy4towm3t9\">Problem</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> It’s a cold winter day, and the weather forecast is predicting the biggest snowstorm in 15 years. Meteorologists are recommending that people stay off the highways and work from home. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> You live on a giant hill and don’t own an all-wheel-drive vehicle, so you’re most likely stuck inside your house anyway when the storm hits. Luckily, you’re a freelancer. Your commute is down the stairs and to the right. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.d58r9vl7xvco\">Agitation</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Except your power is known to be a problem, especially in the winter. About an hour before you’re about to give an important copy presentation, the lights start flickering and BOOM, your power is out. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Meaning? Your Internet is out—no Zoom call for you today. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.yo47oa8ol4v\">Solution</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Note: This exact situation hasn’t happened to me yet, but I know it’s coming considering my power goes out all. the. time. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> So what would I do? \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.s4oyf2kbe0tp\">1. Keep an eye on the weather</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Simple enough, right? You can do this by watching the local news, using a mobile app, or listening to an \n<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/s?k=all+hazards+radio&amp;ref=nb_sb_noss_1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">all-hazards radio</a>&nbsp;if the power is already out. I like to go to the source and read \n<a href=\"https://alerts.weather.gov/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">National Weather Service alerts</a>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.yx6dj8bjkd57\">2. Have a backup mode of communication with my clients (and another backup to the backup)</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> If I think that the weather is going to be a problem, I reach out to my clients in advance to figure out an alternative mode of communication. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:image --> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img alt=\"\" />\n</figure> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":25076} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img class=\"wp-image-25076\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-27-at-8.26.16-PM.png?resize=800%2C288&amp;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-27-at-8.26.16-PM.png?resize=800%2C288&amp;ssl=1 800w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-27-at-8.26.16-PM.png?resize=300%2C108&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-27-at-8.26.16-PM.png?resize=150%2C54&amp;ssl=1 150w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-27-at-8.26.16-PM.png?resize=768%2C277&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-03-27-at-8.26.16-PM.png?w=944&amp;ssl=1 944w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" />\n </figure> \n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> To make sure my cell phone doesn’t lose power, I keep it on the charger AND make sure I have a \n<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/s?k=battery+packs+for+cell+phones&amp;crid=12TC7CGR0GPTD&amp;sprefix=battery+pack%2Caps%2C209&amp;ref=nb_sb_ss_i_4_12\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">battery pack charged</a>&nbsp;in case the call runs long. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.ab8rmdxxmgks\">3. Buy a generator</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> In this scenario, the power may be out…but the Internet likely isn’t. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> So my husband and I finally took the plunge and \n<a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/s?k=generator&amp;ref=nb_sb_noss_2\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">bought a generator</a>&nbsp;to run the electrical circuits to our router during a power outage. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> I don’t recommend doing this unless you have a family member or friend who knows something about wiring electricity, but it’s worth mentioning. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.br42o6rjn7id\">To sum it up</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Hazards like snowstorms, hurricanes, tornadoes, and earthquakes are going to happen… but it’s ultimately up to you to control how they affect your business. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> In general, this scenario is all about staying aware of what’s going on with where you live and making sure you have a backup plan if your Internet, power, or software tools stop working. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading --> \n<h2 id=\"h.8yrqamaplkv\">THREE: There is an external threat to your business’s money or assets</h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<em>Something like: Equipment theft, an IRS tax audit, or a business deal goes south.</em> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.85ichym8ibp2\">Problem</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> You’re an aspiring copywriter who wants to get a few clients under your belt. After creating a \n<a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2014/12/how-to-earn-on-elance/\">profile on Upwork</a>, you score your first gig with an agency! You’re excited to start…but the contract they sent over is full of typos. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.oyt2okcraeha\">Agitation</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> To make sure you’re doing the right thing, you ask a close friend to look over the contract. Meanwhile, the agency needs to run a background check and asks you to scan in your driver’s license and your social security card. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> When your friend Googles the agency, they find reviews of people who say there’s no work available, and it’s all a scam to steal your identity. You immediately stop contact…but they already have your information. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.n3amxz44bj61\">Solution</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> A friend of mine went through this situation when she was looking for temp work after finishing graduate school. Luckily she never got as far as giving out her social security number, but what if she had? \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Here’s what I’d do if this happened to me… \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.jqf91n2dwizw\">1. Turn on credit monitoring</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> You can do a lot with a driver’s license and a social security number, so I’d personally be on the lookout for whether \n<a href=\"https://www.thebalance.com/best-credit-monitoring-services-4164937\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">new credit card accounts get opened in your name</a>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.nswovy6vcmbv\">2. Change your passwords</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Did you know that an email address and password are only worth about \n<a href=\"https://www.keepersecurity.com/how-much-is-my-information-worth-to-hacker-dark-web.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">$</a>\n<a href=\"https://www.keepersecurity.com/how-much-is-my-information-worth-to-hacker-dark-web.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">2.30 on the dark web</a>?&nbsp;So basically, if a cybercriminal has some of your personal identifying information (Like a driver’s license or a social security number), they can pay someone for the other data needed to go on a major shopping spree. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":25069} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img class=\"wp-image-25069\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-04-12-at-2.38.37-PM.png?resize=800%2C377&amp;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-04-12-at-2.38.37-PM.png?resize=800%2C377&amp;ssl=1 800w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-04-12-at-2.38.37-PM.png?resize=300%2C141&amp;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-04-12-at-2.38.37-PM.png?resize=150%2C71&amp;ssl=1 150w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-04-12-at-2.38.37-PM.png?resize=768%2C361&amp;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-04-12-at-2.38.37-PM.png?resize=1536%2C723&amp;ssl=1 1536w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-04-12-at-2.38.37-PM.png?w=1600&amp;ssl=1 1600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" />\n </figure> \n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<img alt=\"\" />\n<em>Source: </em>\n<em><a href=\"https://www.keepersecurity.com/assets/pdf/infographic-how-cybercriminals-make-money.pdf\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Keeper Security</a></em> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> In general, it’s not a bad idea to check that all your online accounts all have unique, \n<a href=\"https://www.forbes.com/sites/kevinmurnane/2019/04/21/how-to-create-unique-passwords-for-every-account-that-are-hard-to-guess-and-easy-to-remember/#d90a2ce1da15\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">hard-to-guess passwords</a>. I like to keep mine in a password safe like \n<a href=\"https://1password.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">1Password</a>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.t91gkrr149ei\">3. Get a really good lawyer</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> It’s nice when your friends are willing to read over your business contracts, but it’s nicer when that friend happens to be a lawyer. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Why? Because they know what red flags to look for. I’ll never forget what a friend once told me about using a lawyer to review contracts… \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<em>It’s not that I don’t trust [them]. It’s that I don’t <strong>want</strong>&nbsp;to trust [them].</em> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> For more on picking out a lawyer for your business, check out these Copywriter Club podcast episodes with legal experts \n<a href=\"https://thecopywriterclub.com/contracts-privacy-christina-scalera/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Christina Scalera</a>&nbsp;and \n<a href=\"https://thecopywriterclub.com/copywriting-legal-questions-danielle-liss/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Danielle Liss</a>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.68d354afwc7k\">To sum this up</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> The work we do as freelancers on the Internet makes us highly susceptible to cybercrime like this scenario. Therefore, it’s worthwhile to take a look at what you’re doing to make sure your information (and your clients’ information) is secure. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> I like this \n<a href=\"https://techlore.tech/securityguide.pdf\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">checklist from Techlore</a>&nbsp;if you’re looking for ideas on how to protect your business. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading --> \n<h2 id=\"h.ku3tsivq1ul\">FOUR: You are under government order to stay where you are</h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<em>Something like: An active shooter event, terrorist event, biological agent attack or pandemic.</em> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> (AKA everything you wish you’d known a month ago.) \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.ofjmtjwjkfrc\">Problem</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> A few dozen elderly patients at a long-term care facility 5 miles from your house develop symptoms of a new flu-like virus with no known cure. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> You’re concerned and make a point to avoid running errands in the area, but it doesn’t necessarily affect your business since you have clients from all around the world. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.d6r64y23ip1b\">Agitation</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> The local school district shuts down after officials discover that students from some of the high schools regularly volunteer at the same long-term care facility. Because it’s not clear how the virus spreads, they switch all their students to telelearning. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> All of a sudden, you’re not just juggling client work – you’re now homeschooling your kids. Also weirdly enough, there’s no toilet paper to be found anywhere. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.b5gokiazfte6\">Solution</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> I do live 5 miles away from \n<a href=\"https://www.seattletimes.com/seattle-news/life-care-center-of-kirkland-the-epicenter-of-seattle-area-coronavirus-outbreak-faces-611000-fine-for-jeopardy-to-patients/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">THE long-term care facility</a>&nbsp;in Washington state, but luckily, my daughter is only a year old, meaning her “curriculum” is more songs and fingerplays. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Which is already overwhelming. So imagine if she had real school. With \n<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/j0SF9pwqK3s\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">classes and homework.</a> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Here’s what I’d do… \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.9dmy954ak4r6\">1. Outsource whatever you can</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> You still need to do the stuff that makes your household run. So let \n<a href=\"https://news.instacart.com/the-instacart-effect-giving-grocers-and-the-economy-a-boost-1315350a7ac7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Instacart</a>&nbsp;deal with finding toilet paper, yeast, or whatever else people are stockpiling. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Plus, you’re giving work to people who need it right now. Just make sure to set up a \n<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sjDuwc9KBps&amp;app=desktop\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">sanitization station.</a> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.vchxzvo5kw07\">2. Block your calendar</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> I’m complete crap at this, so I’ll defer to the experts: \n<a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2016/11/note-to-self-on-time-management/\">Jo herself</a>&nbsp;and \n<a href=\"https://nikkielbaz.com/frum-sanity-webinar/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">this awesome webinar Nikki Elbaz put together</a>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.uvgemfgfliws\">3. Stay as healthy as possible</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> This is a pandemic, people. Meaning that even if you don’t have the killer virus, you want to avoid going to the emergency room. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> So take your vitamins. Stock up on over-the-counter medications like Tylenol and Benadryl. Learn \n<a href=\"http://www.health.gov.on.ca/en/pro/programs/publichealth/coronavirus/docs/2019_primary_care_guidance.pdf\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">some basic first aid.</a>&nbsp;Basically, do whatever you can to avoid physically going to the doctor. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.6jsq1nd96py8\">To sum it all up</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Pandemics are hard to take seriously because they only happen \n<a href=\"https://virus.stanford.edu/uda/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">every hundred years</a>. You can’t see them, and nothing can be done to prevent the spread of disease beyond washing your hands a ton and avoiding close contact with people. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> However. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> The benefit of a pandemic is that there is advance notice, so it’s never a bad idea to stay updated on the news around the world and prepare for a “stay at home” scenario by \n<a href=\"https://www.ready.gov/kit\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">stocking up on extra food, water, and other supplies.</a> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> As for the sudden switch to telemedicine and K-12 distance learning…never in a million years would I have written that into a tabletop exercise. Well played, COVID-19. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading --> \n<h2 id=\"h.l7s51m60nbjf\">Scenario #5: You lose work or can’t land work due to economic conditions</h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<em>Something like: Economic recession, deflation, or inflation</em> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Again, we have real-life to draw inspiration from! \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.s1ppifyboak1\">Problem</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> A killer virus with no known cure infects hundreds of thousands of people around the world, putting all financial markets around the world into a recession. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> You’re concerned, but you’ve positioned yourself as an industry expert and have delivered great wins for your clients. But now you’re not sure if it’s the right time to \n<a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2016/11/quote-higher-rates/\">raise your rates</a>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.vx4g4ax3pwxc\">Agitation</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Your long-time client sends you a Slack message, asking you to meet outside your regularly scheduled time. You later find out that their major investors have pulled out, meaning they can no longer afford your services. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} --> \n<h3 id=\"h.1n07zl6xqop4\">Solution</h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> I hate to be the pessimist here, but this could happen to any of us in the next coming weeks. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Read on for some ideas on what you can do to keep your business afloat. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.dbv02ax4zhrg\">1. Expand your niche</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Remember all that advice about \n<a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2016/11/find-your-niche/\">finding your niche</a>? It works like crazy during a period of economic prosperity…but it might not work as well if the industry you picked is crumbling as we speak. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> So think outside the box. What other experiences can you draw from that could help people right now? Do your current clients need additional services beyond copywriting? \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> It’s not an ideal situation, but it’s something that could help you pay the bills IF you needed it. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.lv3hvjpoy2gz\">2. Go through every business expense and ask yourself, “Do I need this?”</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Yeah, I know it’s boring. But every transaction matters right now. If your boat were sinking, you’d start throwing non-essential items overboard. The same goes for your business. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> You can import your transactions into a tool like \n<a href=\"https://www.mint.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Mint</a>&nbsp;or \n<a href=\"https://www.quicken.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Quicken</a>&nbsp;for further analysis. But honestly, I prefer to print out my bank and credit card statements and go through them with a highlighter. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":25073} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img class=\"wp-image-25073\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/northfolk-Ok76F6yW2iA-unsplash.jpg?resize=800%2C450&amp;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/northfolk-Ok76F6yW2iA-unsplash.jpg?resize=800%2C450&amp;ssl=1 800w, \n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<em>Source: </em>\n<em><a href=\"https://unsplash.com/s/photos/budget?utm_source=unsplash&amp;utm_medium=referral&amp;utm_content=creditCopyText\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">NORTHFOLK on Unsplash</a></em> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4} --> \n<h4 id=\"h.2x4uqrw24blc\">3. Apply for financial assistance with the Small Business Association (SBA)</h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> If all else fails and you need to cover payroll or other expenses sooner than later, the \n<a href=\"https://www.uschamber.com/report/guide-sbas-economic-injury-disaster-loans\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Small Business Association can help</a>. Some of them are grants; some of them are loans. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Obviously, read the fine print. If your business strapped for cash, there is no shame in asking for help. That’s what the government does best in an emergency. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading --> \n<h2 id=\"h.xmgxk3kweqqd\">Now it’s your turn</h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> You and I could come up with scenarios all day even worse than reality (\n<a href=\"https://www.cdc.gov/cpr/zombie/index.htm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Zombies, anyone?</a>). Still, it doesn’t change the fact that as a copywriter, you already have the skills you need to survive your first recession, pandemic, or any other disaster that could put you out of business. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> By simply using the \n<strong>Problem, Agitation, Solution</strong>&nbsp;formula, you can walk through almost any situation and figure out ways you might prepare or respond to them. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Again, the \n<strong>5 types of emergency scenarios</strong>&nbsp;are… \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true} --> \n<ol> \n <li>You can’t work for an extended period</li> \n <li>The physical place you work is malfunctioning or uninhabitable</li> \n <li>External threats to your business assets</li> \n <li>You are under government order to stay where you are</li> \n <li>You lose work or can’t find work due to economic conditions</li> \n</ol> \n<!-- /wp:list --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> And if you’re still not convinced this exercise is worth the time, keep in mind that \n<a href=\"https://www.fema.gov/media-library/assets/documents/108451\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">40-60% of businesses never reopen after a disaster.</a> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Besides time, what do you have to lose – especially if it could prevent your career as a freelance copywriter from becoming part of a statistic? \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Give it a try, come up with your own scenarios, and let me know what you think. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Stay safe, \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> Sophia \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<strong>P.S.</strong>&nbsp;Struggling to figure out what you \n<strong>actually need</strong>&nbsp;to get your business prepared for an emergency? I’m working on a \n<strong>checklist</strong>&nbsp;for you. \n<a href=\"https://sophia-le.ck.page/469994f7dd\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Sign up here to get notified when it’s live</a>. \n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n<script type=\"text/javascript\"> window.rmpanda = window.rmpanda || {}; window.rmpanda.wpvars = window.rmpanda.wpvars || {}; var debug = (window.rmpanda || 00%2C288&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn42@2020_4/2020/08/25/02-39-08-353_c791de46aaa7442a.webp","https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Screen-Shot-2020-04-12-at-2.38.37-PM.png?resize=800%2C377&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn94@2020_5/2020/08/25/02-39-02-447_1ff4b18f978a8d98.webp","https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/northfolk-Ok76F6yW2iA-unsplash.jpg?resize=800%2C450&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn50@2020_2/2020/08/25/02-39-01-136_9cdc66594b472752.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598323135051},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 10:38:55","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 10:38:55","title":"You Don’t Need Ads on Your Site to Monetize Your Blog. Here’s How Bloggers Make Six Figures.","link":"https://copyhackers.com/?p=24572","description":"\n<p class=\"has-text-color has-small-font-size has-cyan-bluish-gray-color\">LAST UPDATED AUGUST 14, 2020</p>\n\n\n\n<p>They say hard work is a reward unto itself.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But for most freelancers &#8211; you know, the kind with bills and a constant eye on their bank balance &#8211; it’s a lot more rewarding when work turns into hard cash.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Let’s face it: There’re only so many pats on the back you can survive on when you’re trying to make money from your blog. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Like, five. Maybe seven, tops.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/1.gif?ssl=1\" alt=\"Saturday Night Live gif congratulations\" class=\"wp-image-25134\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Eventually, probably sooner rather than later, you need to take those pats on the back and turn them into bank account deposits.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>In other words, you need to monetize your blog.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You don’t have to go far to find the supposed secret to making money from a blog, either: shake a stick at Google, and you’ll find plenty of people promising that paid ads are your golden ticket to blogging for money.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Take <a href=\"https://www.ryrob.com/about/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">Ryan Robinson</a>, for example, who’s taught over 400,000 monthly readers how to start a blog. In his words:&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>“Displaying advertisement space is arguably the easiest, most basic (and quickest) form of starting to make money blogging.”</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<p>And if you check out the number of ad buyers who partake in Google AdSense (one of the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.webfx.com/internet-marketing/top-display-ad-networks.html\" target=\"_blank\">largest display ad networks</a>), you’ll notice an <a href=\"https://trends.builtwith.com/ads/Google-Adsense\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">upward trend</a> for usage.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/2.png?ssl=1\" alt=\"Google Adsense Usage Statistics\" class=\"wp-image-25136\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/2.png?w=766&#38;ssl=1 766w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/2.png?resize=300%2C250&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/2.png?resize=150%2C125&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 766px) 100vw, 766px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>HOWEVER, <em>also </em>in blog guru <a href=\"https://www.ryrob.com/make-money-blogging/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">Ryan Robinson</a>’s words:</p>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>“Of all the different ways to make money blogging that I&#8217;m engaged in, [running ads] is one of the <strong>lowest returns </strong>in terms of total dollars earned (especially for my amount of traffic).”</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<p>With over 2.4 million readers last year, Ryan has the numbers to optimize ad payouts.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li></li></ul>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/3.png?resize=766%2C324&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Ryan Robinson's Blog Traffic\" class=\"wp-image-25139\" width=\"766\" height=\"324\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/3.png?w=766&#38;ssl=1 766w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/3.png?resize=300%2C127&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/3.png?resize=150%2C63&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 766px) 100vw, 766px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Ryan Robinson&#8217;s Blog Traffic</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>You need a minimum of <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.adthrive.com/faqs/\" target=\"_blank\">100,000 monthly pageviews</a> to join AdThrive’s network and <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.mediavine.com/mediavine-requirements-why-our-application-process-yields-the-best-results/\" target=\"_blank\">25,000 monthly sessions</a> (around 30,000 pageviews) for Mediavine (there’s no minimum for AdSense and Sovrn).</p>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">And that’s <strong>still not enough</strong>. These days, to earn $100,000 a year through Google AdSense, you need approximately <a href=\"https://www.minterest.com/how-much-traffic-do-you-need-to-make-money/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">20,000 visitors a day</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p><em>Sheesh.</em></p>\n\n\n\n<p>So, if you see someone bragging about the revenue power of ads like this recommendation from <a href=\"https://problogger.com/adsense/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">ProBlogger</a>:&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>“<strong>AdSense is how I earn around 35% of my income </strong>as a full-time blogger and I would thoroughly recommend it as a way of monetizing a blog &#8211; especially for those just starting out.”&#160;</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<p>&#8230;dig a little deeper and check the fine print (a.k.a., the date) like in the comments of ProBlogger founder Darren Rowse’s <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://problogger.com/adsense-tips-for-bloggers-1/\" target=\"_blank\">AdSense Tips article</a>, which were published in &#8211; wait for it &#8211; 2009.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/4.png?resize=751%2C456&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Check the dates ProBlogger\" class=\"wp-image-25140\" width=\"751\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/4.png?w=751&#38;ssl=1 751w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/4.png?resize=300%2C182&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/4.png?resize=150%2C91&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 751px) 100vw, 751px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Check the dates</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><em>BRIEF INTERRUPTION: We lurve Problogger around here. This is nothing against Problogger! Just a reminder to always check the dates when grabbing tips from the interwebs. Now, back to our regularly scheduled programming&#8230;</em></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Needless to say, decade-old enthusiasm isn’t very reliable.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But okay. Let’s ignore the outdated advice for a minute. Say someone &#8211; someone with a pretty website and tons of widgets &#8211; says ad revenue brings in <a href=\"https://brandongaille.com/blog-income-report-study/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">35% of their blog earnings</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>(Or, just say they’re someone who took the below survey&#8230;)</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/5.png?resize=641%2C379&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"2018 Blog Income Report Research Study by The Blog Millionaire\" class=\"wp-image-25141\" width=\"641\" height=\"379\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/5.png?w=641&#38;ssl=1 641w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/5.png?resize=300%2C177&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/5.png?resize=150%2C89&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 641px) 100vw, 641px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>2018 Blog Income Report Research Study by The Blog Millionaire</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Well, there’s fine print there, too.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">If they make that much money with their blog, they’re hardly a beginner blogger. More likely, they&#8217;re an uber large publisher with <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.viglink.com/blog/2017/05/15/state-affiliate-marketing-survey/\" target=\"_blank\">over 100,000 unique monthly views</a>. This report entirely omits bloggers who make less than $2,000 per month (which, in reality, is the <a href=\"https://www.blogtyrant.com/new-blogging-statistics/\">majority of bloggers</a>).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>What’s more is that when you get into the <em>really</em> high income levels (over $25,000 per month), blogger income from ad revenue <a href=\"https://brandongaille.com/blog-income-report-study/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">dramatically drops to 3%</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/6.png?resize=638%2C378&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"2018 Blog Income Report Research Study by The Blog Millionaire\" class=\"wp-image-25142\" width=\"638\" height=\"378\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/6.png?w=638&#38;ssl=1 638w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/6.png?resize=300%2C178&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/6.png?resize=150%2C89&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 638px) 100vw, 638px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>2018 Blog Income Report Research Study by The Blog Millionaire</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Oh, and there’s one other teensy-weensy thing:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>People <em>don’t like </em>ads.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I mean, look at the masses of online users who <strong>actively block ads</strong>. A chunky <a href=\"https://www.emarketer.com/content/demanding-a-better-ad-experience\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">25% of U.S. Internet users</a> actively avoid giving ads the time of day.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/7.png?resize=494%2C473&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: eMarketer Report - Demanding a Better Ad Experience\" class=\"wp-image-25143\" width=\"494\" height=\"473\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/7.png?w=494&#38;ssl=1 494w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/7.png?resize=300%2C287&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/7.png?resize=150%2C144&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 494px) 100vw, 494px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: eMarketer Report &#8211; Demanding a Better Ad Experience</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And &#8211; just in case that simple truth isn’t enough &#8211; there is an onslaught of <a href=\"https://www.magnet4blogging.net/adsense-is-bad-idea/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">cons to putting ads on your blog</a>:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Ads dilute your brand</li><li>Ads take up too much real estate on your page</li><li>Ads distract your reader and kill your conversions&#160;</li><li>Ads increase your load time</li><li>Ads ruin your trust factor</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>So, the jury is in:</strong> Unless you have a blog that pulls in over 100,000 monthly views, paid ads aren’t the best way to make money online. They aren’t even a <em>good </em>way to do it.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/8.gif?ssl=1\" alt=\"Conan O'Brien GIF womp womp\" class=\"wp-image-25144\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Where does that leave the hopeful blogger who wants to translate their adoring fans into adorable revenue streams?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>In a much better place than you’d think, actually.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 class=\"has-text-align-center\">How much money can you make by monetizing your blog without using ads?</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>In short, you can earn more than six times the average annual income in the U.S. (which was logged at <a href=\"https://www.thebalance.com/what-is-average-income-in-usa-family-household-history-3306189\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">$31,786 per capita</a> in 2017).&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If we’re talking freelance copywriter salaries, that’s <em>triple</em> the average amount that <a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2016/11/freelance-copywriters-share-how-much-money-they-earn/#question11\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">50% of freelance copywriters expect to earn</a> (which is less than $50,000 annually).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>That’s right &#8211; pro bloggers can rake in an <a href=\"https://convertkit.com/reports/blogging/money\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">average annual revenue of $185,975</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/9.png?resize=579%2C535&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: ConvertKit's 2017 State of the Blogging Industry Report\" class=\"wp-image-25145\" width=\"579\" height=\"535\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/9.png?w=579&#38;ssl=1 579w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/9.png?resize=300%2C277&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/9.png?resize=150%2C139&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 579px) 100vw, 579px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>ConvertKit&#8217;s 2017 State of the Blogging Industry Report</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And if you’re <em>really </em>good, you can hit the six-figure mark on a MONTHLY basis.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Need proof?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>In less than six years, Michelle Gardner, who runs the Making Sense Of Cents blog, one of the most successful monetized blogs out there, earns over <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://blossomthemes.com/top-earning-blogs/\" target=\"_blank\">$126,000 in monthly revenue</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/10.png?resize=653%2C264&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: 22 Wildly-Successful Bloggers Who Make Thousands of Dollars Every Month\" class=\"wp-image-25146\" width=\"653\" height=\"264\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/10.png?w=653&#38;ssl=1 653w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/10.png?resize=300%2C121&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/10.png?resize=150%2C61&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 653px) 100vw, 653px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: 22 Wildly-Successful Bloggers Who Make Thousands of Dollars Every Month</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">Impressive, right? But far from the top-of-class results.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>John Lee Dumas, founder of Entrepreneurs on Fire, has grossed <a href=\"https://www.eofire.com/income/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">over $1.5 million</a> for the year so far.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And totaled $16,204,901 in blog revenue since he launched in 2012 &#8211; wowsa.&#160;&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/11.png?resize=519%2C568&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Entrepreneurs on Fire Monthly Income Report\" class=\"wp-image-25147\" width=\"519\" height=\"568\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/11.png?w=519&#38;ssl=1 519w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/11.png?resize=274%2C300&#38;ssl=1 274w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/11.png?resize=137%2C150&#38;ssl=1 137w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 519px) 100vw, 519px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Entrepreneurs on Fire Monthly Income Report</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Did you notice any of his blog revenue flowing in from ads?&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Didn’t think so.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Okay, so maybe you’re thinking, <em>I don’t have six-plus years to dedicate solely to growing my blog.</em></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Totally normal. These are superstar-status bloggers.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>(Plus, you need to run your freelance business, right?)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But that’s not to say you can’t make money blogging as a normal human-status blogger.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You can. You totally can.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But not without some serious commitment.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Skip the commitment, and you&#8217;re likely to end up as one of the <a href=\"https://www.blogtyrant.com/new-blogging-statistics/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">69.4% of bloggers</a> who make zilch.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>That’s right &#8211; the majority of bloggers don’t make any money at all.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/12.png?resize=636%2C448&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Blog Tyrant's BIG Blogging Survey\" class=\"wp-image-25148\" width=\"636\" height=\"448\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/12.png?w=636&#38;ssl=1 636w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/12.png?resize=300%2C211&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/12.png?resize=150%2C106&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 636px) 100vw, 636px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Blog Tyrant&#8217;s BIG Blogging Survey</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Why? Among other things, because they didn’t put in the commitment &#8211; <a href=\"https://www.blogtyrant.com/new-blogging-statistics/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">59.3% of bloggers</a> start a blog and then abandon it.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/13.png?resize=472%2C195&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Blog Tyrant's BIG Blogging Survey\" class=\"wp-image-25149\" width=\"472\" height=\"195\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/13.png?w=472&#38;ssl=1 472w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/13.png?resize=300%2C124&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/13.png?resize=150%2C62&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/13.png?resize=470%2C195&#38;ssl=1 470w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 472px) 100vw, 472px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>To<em> </em>make money blogging, it’s likely to take <a href=\"https://amylynnandrews.com/how-to-make-money-blogging/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">a year to reach part-time income levels</a>. For full-time income levels, double that timeframe.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Okay, so blog monetization is great, but not so easy-peasy.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Let’s make sure you’re in the minority here and tackle <em>when</em> to monetize.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 class=\"has-text-align-center\">When should you monetize your blog?</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>The short answer: monetize your audience when you’ve established your blog and have a growing fanbase.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Like most everything, the long answer comes with more deets.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Does size matter? Of course it does.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Naturally, the bigger your following, the higher your chances of earning a significant income. Critical mass is a real thing. Check it out:</p>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/grow-blog-subscribers-grow-traffic\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">75% of the traffic</a> and 90% of the leads HubSpot pulls in on its blog each month actually come from posts that <em>weren&#8217;t </em>published that month.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/14.png?resize=609%2C544&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Want More Blog traffic? Focus on Growing Subscribers - HubSpot\" class=\"wp-image-25150\" width=\"609\" height=\"544\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/14.png?w=609&#38;ssl=1 609w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/14.png?resize=300%2C268&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/14.png?resize=150%2C134&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 609px) 100vw, 609px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Want More Blog traffic? Focus on Growing Subscribers &#8211; HubSpot</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>When you hit critical mass levels, your <strong>older content</strong> starts working for you, spurring exponential growth like HubSpot’s 2011 and 2012 jumps in blog subscribership and blog traffic.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But is it a requirement to have a large following? Not at all.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You can start monetizing your blog as soon as you have your foundation laid out and a growing (even if slowly) subscriber list.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Seems straightforward enough.</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Here’s the catch: </strong>You need to be willing to commit designated time to create content. And not just dropping an article or two from time to time. You need to <strong><em>publish consistently.</em></strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Why? Because that’s how you grow and sustain that growth. There’s no way around it.</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>So&#8230;how often should you blog?</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Brands that publish over 16 posts each month get nearly <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/blogging-frequency-benchmarks\">3.5 times more traffic</a> than companies that publish zero to four monthly blog posts. (Is it good traffic? Is it returning traffic? That&#8217;s the topic of another post! One thing at a time.)</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/15.png?resize=595%2C332&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: How Often Should Companies Blog - HubSpot\" class=\"wp-image-25151\" width=\"595\" height=\"332\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/15.png?w=595&#38;ssl=1 595w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/15.png?resize=300%2C168&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/15.png?resize=150%2C84&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/15.png?resize=215%2C120&#38;ssl=1 215w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/15.png?resize=414%2C232&#38;ssl=1 414w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 595px) 100vw, 595px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Beyond traffic, your blog frequency also affects the number of leads you pull in. If you’re a company with one to 10 employees (and as a freelancer, you probably are), sources say you’ll benefit the most by blogging more than <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/blogging-frequency-benchmarks\" target=\"_blank\">10 times per month</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/16.png?resize=603%2C333&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: How Often Should Companies Blog - HubSpot\" class=\"wp-image-25152\" width=\"603\" height=\"333\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/16.png?w=603&#38;ssl=1 603w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/16.png?resize=300%2C166&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/16.png?resize=150%2C83&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/16.png?resize=215%2C120&#38;ssl=1 215w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 603px) 100vw, 603px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: How Often Should Companies Blog &#8211; HubSpot</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3>And&#8230;how long should your blog posts be?</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>As far as blog post length goes, the optimal word count has been getting longer and longer. The average blog post ranges from <a href=\"https://www.searchmetrics.com/knowledge-base/ranking-factors/\">1,140 to 1,285 words</a>, so the rule has become to shoot for at least that.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>To hit the top 10 positions in search rankings though, you’ll want to write even longer.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/17.png?resize=800%2C422&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Longer content = better search rankings\" class=\"wp-image-25153\" width=\"800\" height=\"422\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/17.png?resize=800%2C422&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/17.png?resize=300%2C158&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/17.png?resize=150%2C79&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/17.png?resize=768%2C405&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/17.png?w=871&#38;ssl=1 871w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Longer content = better search rankings</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>If writing upwards of 2,450 words per post sounds overwhelming to you, you don’t have to leave your freelance blog monetizing dreams behind just yet. <em>Shorter posts work well for different purposes.&#160;</em></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Case in point:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>For more comments on your freelance blog, discussion-based posts with 275 words work well, like this post with <a href=\"https://thewritepractice.com/strongest-characterization/\">over 300 comments</a>.</li><li>For more social shares, aim for the <a href=\"https://thewritepractice.com/blog-post-length/\">1,000 to 1,500 word range</a>.&#160;</li><li>The perfect blog post length <a href=\"https://moz.com/blog/blog-post-length-frequency\">may not even exist</a>.</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>The moral here is: </strong>Aim to write at least 10 blog posts each month at 1,000+ words per post. If you’ve got the people-power to pump out more content, do it. And if you can write <a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/how-to-write-an-epic-blog-post/\">epic blog posts</a>, (obviously) do that, too.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Sound doable? Then so will what’s next.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2 class=\"has-text-align-center\">Best Blog Monetization Tactics <br>That Are Actually Doable<strong>&#160;</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Once you’re churning out content on the regular and building a solid audience, you’re ready to take it to the next level. So let’s get monetizing&#8230;</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>Write Sponsored Blog Posts and Product Reviews</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>One way to leverage your blog audience is to connect with companies that will pay you to either:&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Write a post about a relevant topic that includes a nestled link to their site (a sponsored post) or&#160;</li><li>Review one of their products and services in your article (a product review).&#160;&#160;</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>For a real life example, check out Lou Martin, a pro blogger, in action on her <a href=\"https://www.productreviewmom.com/2019/09/after-huge-setback-updating-my-hair.html\">Product Review Mom</a> blog.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/18.png?resize=800%2C547&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"product review\" class=\"wp-image-25154\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/18.png?resize=800%2C547&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/18.png?resize=300%2C205&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/18.png?resize=150%2C103&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/18.png?resize=768%2C525&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/18.png?resize=990%2C677&#38;ssl=1 990w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/18.png?resize=379%2C259&#38;ssl=1 379w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/18.png?w=1100&#38;ssl=1 1100w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Lou gets paid anywhere from $200 to $500 per post review.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If that sounds like pennies to you, think again. She does this full-time while raising two teen girls. It adds up quick. Three to four quick reviews a week could give her full-time income. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Why does this blog monetization tip work so well?&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>With your growing audience comes a <a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2016/11/find-your-niche/\">niche market</a> that other relevant brands and organizations want to tap into. They’ll pay you to access your like-minded audience.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Lou has drummed up a healthy niche audience that attracts large brand partners such as Disney, Nickelodeon, Neutrogena and more. She’s even got her <a href=\"https://www.productreviewmom.com/p/be-guest.html\">audience demo info</a> sorted out for partners to scan for a match.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/19.png?resize=800%2C620&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Lou Martins Blog Audience Demographics\" class=\"wp-image-25155\" posts, though &#8211; <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://shanebarker.com/blog/influencer-marketing-statistics/\" target=\"_blank\">54% of them</a> leverage their audiences and partake in publishing sponsored posts.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/20.png?resize=679%2C407&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: 85 Influencer Marketing Statistics that Will Surprise you in 2018 - Shane Barker Blog</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>The better you are at promoting sponsored posts and the more consistent you are at churning them out, the better your paycheck will be.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If you take a closer look at John Lee Dumas’s Entrepreneurs on Fire blog, the largest portion of his revenue currently comes from his <a href=\"https://www.eofire.com/income/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">sponsorship arrangements</a>.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 610px) 100vw, 610px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Entrepreneurs on Fire Income Report</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>As for what you can charge for sponsored posts, it runs the gamut.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Annabel Candy, a seasoned 17-year blogger and original founder of SuccessfulBlogging, charges <a href=\"https://www.successfulblogging.com/sponsored-blog-post-rates/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">over $700 for a sponsored blog post</a>.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Ryan Robinson is another pro blogger who charges <a href=\"https://www.ryrob.com/how-start-blog/#11\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">$1,500 per sponsored post</a>.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>AuthorityHacker earns <a href=\"https://www.authorityhacker.com/how-to-write-product-reviews-that-sell/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">three to five figures in revenue</a> for publishing reviews, as you can see in this 12-month earnings snapshot.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/22.png?resize=789%2C429&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Authority Hacker 12-month Earnings Report\" class=\"wp-image-25158\" width=\"789\" height=\"429\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/22.png?w=789&#38;ssl=1 789w,
