Hacker 12-month Earnings Report</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Naturally, the more your audience grows, the more you have to leverage per sponsored post and review.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If you’re looking for ways to review products and secure sponsored posts, scope out some of these sites:&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://freelancewritersden.com/affiliates/\" target=\"_blank\">Freelance Writers Den</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://prowritingaid.com/en/Affiliate/Program\" target=\"_blank\">ProWritingAid</a></li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>And if you want to copywrite for your clients and help <em>them</em> promote affiliate products, there’s a near-endless supply of affiliate marketing programs to peruse:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://try.activate.social/\" target=\"_blank\">Activate</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.bzzagent.com/\" target=\"_blank\">BzzAgent</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.infolinks.com/join-us/\" target=\"_blank\">Infolinks</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.tomoson.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Tomoson</a></li><li><a href=\"https://www.influenster.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">Influenster</a></li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>But if that doesn’t suit your (or your client’s) brand, our next monetizing method might be more your speed.</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>Partner Up with Affiliates to Monetize Your Blog</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Another monetizing option is to connect with affiliates. Just like sponsored posts, affiliate blogging also involves hooking up with like-minded peeps.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The difference here is you’re paid a commission fee every time one of your readers purchases their products from one of your blog links.&#160;&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If you want to keep your integrity high and your reputation unscathed, make sure your affiliate partner sells products and services that your audience <em>actually cares about</em>.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Ask yourself honestly: </strong>Will your audience benefit from your affiliate’s offer?&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Follow in the footsteps of others who do affiliate blogging well. Looping back to Michelle Gardner’s Making Sense of Cents blog, she exclusively promotes <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.makingsenseofcents.com/recommendations\" target=\"_blank\">money-saving sites</a> she believes in.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/23.png?resize=800%2C620&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Money Saving Websites Michelle Gardner Promotes on Her Blog\" class=\"wp-image-25159\" width=\"800\" height=\"620\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/23.png?resize=800%2C620&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/23.png?resize=300%2C233&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/23.png?resize=150%2C116&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/23.png?resize=768%2C595&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/23.png?w=925&#38;ssl=1 925w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Money Saving Websites Michelle Gardner Promotes on Her Blog</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Which keeps her on topic and serving her audience’s interest with <strong>good quality products or services </strong>&#8211; <em>the </em>single top reason <a href=\"https://www.marketingcharts.com/charts/why-consumers-trust-brands/attachment/edelman-why-consumers-trust-brands-jul2019\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">why consumers trust brands</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/24.png?resize=800%2C373&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Why Customer Trust Brands - Marketing Charts\" class=\"wp-image-25160\" width=\"800\" height=\"373\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/24.png?resize=800%2C373&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/24.png?resize=300%2C140&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/24.png?resize=150%2C70&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/24.png?resize=768%2C358&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/24.png?resize=990%2C461&#38;ssl=1 990w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/24.png?w=1028&#38;ssl=1 1028w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Why Customer Trust Brands &#8211; Marketing Charts</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>There’s no need to inundate your following with useless products that won’t serve them. Beyond being an exercise in futility, doing so runs the risk of losing their trust, hands-down the most lethal biz move you can make.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>After all, <a href=\"https://www.visioncritical.com/blog/authenticity-stats\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">63% of customers</a> would only buy from you if they believed you to be authentic and trustworthy.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>On top of that, <a href=\"https://adage.com/article/digital/5-key-takeaways-2019-edelman-brand-trust-survey/2178646\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">81% of consumers</a> “must be able to trust the brand to do what is right.” So don’t blow it. You’ve worked hard at building trust among your blog audience.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Speaking of doing what’s right, it’s a <a href=\"https://www.ftc.gov/tips-advice/business-center/guidance/ftcs-endorsement-guides-what-people-are-asking\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">legal U.S. requirement</a> to disclose any affiliate links included in your blog. Michelle also nails this nicely at the top of her affiliates page.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/25.png?resize=800%2C527&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Michelle Gardner's Affiliate Page\" class=\"wp-image-25161\" width=\"800\" height=\"527\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/25.png?resize=800%2C527&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/25.png?resize=300%2C198&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/25.png?resize=150%2C99&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/25.png?resize=768%2C506&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/25.png?resize=130%2C86&#38;ssl=1 130w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/25.png?resize=187%2C124&#38;ssl=1 187w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/25.png?w=898&#38;ssl=1 898w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Michelle Gardner&#8217;s Affiliate Page</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Okay, now that we’re clear on <em>whom </em>to partner up with (those who warrant trust, of course), on to the payouts for affiliate blogging.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>An average affiliate commission runs between <a href=\"https://cospot.com/affiliate/average-affiliate-commission-rates/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">5% and 30%</a>.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Just like commission rates vary, so do annual affiliate income levels. In one <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://finchsells.com/2013/10/10/how-much-can-you-earn-from-affiliate-marketing/\" target=\"_blank\">poll of 117 bloggers</a>, the annual affiliate revenue ranged from less than $20,000 to over $2 million.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/26.jpg?resize=628%2C278&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"how Much Do You Make Per Year\" class=\"wp-image-25162\" width=\"628\" height=\"278\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/26.jpg?w=628&#38;ssl=1 628w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/26.jpg?resize=300%2C133&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/26.jpg?resize=150%2C66&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 628px) 100vw, 628px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Why is the range so wide? It depends on several factors. The three biggest are:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><strong>Industry</strong> &#8211; Health companies like The Vitamin Shoppe pay out a max of <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.vitaminshoppe.com/lp/affiliate\" target=\"_blank\">9% commission</a>, while marketing SaaS companies like SEMrush pay as much as <a href=\"https://www.berush.com/en/\">40% in recurring commission</a>.</li><li><strong>Product price</strong> &#8211; <em>Generally</em> speaking, <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://cospot.com/affiliate/average-affiliate-commission-rates/\" target=\"_blank\">lower-priced products</a> tend to have higher commission rates and luxury goods often pay out at lower rates, which is why you’ll see a huge range from <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://support.clickbank.com/hc/en-us/articles/220365887-Earning-Commissions-Getting-Paid#How%20Commissions%20are%20Calculated\" target=\"_blank\">1% to 75%</a> on sites like ClickBank.&#160;</li><li><strong>Vendor’s valuation</strong> &#8211; Ultimately, payouts are decided on and <a href=\"https://support.clickbank.com/hc/en-us/articles/220365887-Earning-Commissions-Getting-Paid#How%20Commissions%20are%20Calculated\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">set by the vendor</a>.&#160;</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>The gist of it is: </strong>Payouts vary, so while affiliate blogging can make bank for one creator, it can be more like <em>a piggy bank</em> for another.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Even within a single vertical, the numbers can run WILD. For instance, WordPress products offer an average commission payout of <a href=\"https://www.codeinwp.com/blog/effective-commission-for-a-wordpress-affiliate-program/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">35% for their affiliate programs</a>, but that’s an average with a lot of standard deviation.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/27.png?resize=800%2C352&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: What's the Most Effective Commission Level for a WordPress Affiliate Program - codeinwp\" class=\"wp-image-25163\" width=\"800\" height=\"352\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/27.png?resize=800%2C352&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/27.png?resize=300%2C132&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/27.png?resize=150%2C66&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/27.png?resize=768%2C338&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/27.png?resize=990%2C436&#38;ssl=1 990w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/27.png?w=1020&#38;ssl=1 1020w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: What&#8217;s the Most Effective Commission Level for a WordPress Affiliate Program &#8211; codeinwp</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Let’s zoom out, though, and look at the people behind the numbers.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Can affiliate blogging be a bust? Yes.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Can you still earn a significant income? Double yes.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>As a blogger who partakes heavily in WordPress’s affiliate marketing, Tom Dupuis went from making <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://onlinemediamasters.com/how-to-make-money-with-affiliate-marketing/\" target=\"_blank\">$20,000 to $150,000 within two years</a>. Here’s a snapshot of a month’s worth of <a href=\"https://onlinemediamasters.com/how-to-make-money-with-affiliate-marketing/#reports\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">affiliate income</a> at the end of 2018.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/28.png?resize=689%2C428&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: How to Make Money with Affiliate Marketing (2019 Guide) - Online Media Masters\" class=\"wp-image-25164\" width=\"689\" height=\"428\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/28.png?w=689&#38;ssl=1 689w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/28.png?resize=300%2C186&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/28.png?resize=150%2C93&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 689px) 100vw, 689px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: How to Make Money with Affiliate Marketing (2019 Guide) &#8211; Online Media Masters</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Michelle Gardner attributes <a href=\"https://www.makingsenseofcents.com/2019/09/how-i-made-money-blogging-in-august-2019-my-top-blogging-mistakes.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">63% of her blog income</a> to affiliates (for the month of August 2019) and she earns over $100,000 per month blogging.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/29.png?resize=560%2C465&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: How I Made Money Blogging in August 2019 - Making Sense of Cents\" class=\"wp-image-25167\" width=\"560\" height=\"465\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/29.png?w=560&#38;ssl=1 560w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/29.png?resize=300%2C249&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/29.png?resize=150%2C125&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 560px) 100vw, 560px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: How I Made Money Blogging in August 2019 &#8211; Making Sense of Cents</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>For a star-studded example of how much money you can make from affiliate blogging, look no further than Smart Passive Income’s founder, Pat Flynn.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>He earned <a href=\"https://www.smartpassiveincome.com/affiliate-marketing-strategies/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">$200,000 in commission payments</a> for including a link to an exam software product on his first website <em>almost a decade ago</em>.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Since then, he’s made hundreds of thousands of dollars from affiliate marketing including $300,000 from a single affiliate agreement with ConvertKit.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/30.png?resize=800%2C357&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: How I Earned $300K+ Passive Income from One Product - Smart Passive Income\" class=\"wp-image-25170\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/30.png?resize=800%2C357&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/30.png?resize=300%2C134&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/30.png?resize=150%2C67&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/30.png?resize=768%2C342&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/30.png?resize=990%2C441&#38;ssl=1 990w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/30.png?resize=1320%2C588&#38;ssl=1 1320w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/30.png?w=1353&#38;ssl=1 1353w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: How I Earned $300K+ Passive Income from One Product &#8211; Smart Passive Income</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>And yeah, if you’re wondering, the goods are solid on both sides of the affiliate blogging game &#8211; <a href=\"https://www.viglink.com/blog/2017/05/15/state-affiliate-marketing-survey/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">65% of publishers</a> claim the top benefit to affiliate marketing is generating additional revenue.</p>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">In the U.S. alone, retailers spend nearly <a href=\"https://www.bigcommerce.com/blog/affiliate-marketing/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">$5.5 billion annually</a> on affiliate marketing and a staggering 84% of online publishers use affiliate marketing.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Oh, and unlike paid ads, blog publishers <em>like </em>affiliate marketing &#8211; <a href=\"https://www.viglink.com/blog/2017/05/15/state-affiliate-marketing-survey/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">76% of publishers</a> say affiliate programs make monetizing a cinch and 45% claim it doesn’t disrupt the user experience.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/31.png?ssl=1\" alt=\"From: State of Affiliate Marketing Survey 2017 - Sovrn//Commerce\" class=\"wp-image-25171\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/31.png?w=801&#38;ssl=1 801w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/31.png?resize=300%2C137&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/31.png?resize=150%2C69&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/31.png?resize=768%2C351&#38;ssl=1 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 801px) 100vw, 801px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: State of Affiliate Marketing Survey 2017 &#8211; Sovrn//Commerce</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>With warm and fuzzy sentiments like these, take a gander at some of today’s most popular affiliate programs:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.awin.com/us\" target=\"_blank\">Affiliate Window</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://affiliate-program.amazon.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Amazon Associates</a></li><li><a href=\"https://www.cj.com/\">CJ Affiliate</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.clickbank.com/\" target=\"_blank\">ClickBank</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://partnernetwork.ebay.com/\" target=\"_blank\">eBay Partner Network</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://support.leadpages.net/hc/en-us/articles/360009044771-Leadpages-Affiliate-Partner-Program\" target=\"_blank\">Leadpages Partner Program</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.maxbounty.com/\" target=\"_blank\">MaxBounty</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://rakutenmarketing.com/affiliate\" target=\"_blank\">Rakuten Marketing Affiliates</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.shopify.com/affiliates\" target=\"_blank\">Shopify Affiliate Program</a></li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.tradedoubler.com/en/\" target=\"_blank\">Tradedoubler</a></li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>As you can see, affiliate blogging is a lot like ice cream. There’s an option for every palette and diet.</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>In sum</strong>: Affiliate blogging is a non-intrusive way to serve your readers while making money from said service. Just be sure you can vouch for your affiliate’s offerings.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Our next blog monetizing tactic is also a way to serve your audience with tons of options.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>Productize Your Expertise and Sell a Digital Download to Earn Money Online</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Selling digital downloads is a <em>great</em> way to scale your business without sinking in a ton of time.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Why? Because the majority of your work is done on the front-end. Once you’ve created your digital file and uploaded it to your site, you’ve conquered the uphill portion of the hustle.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>From there, you just need to maintain your marketing.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You don’t have to worry about hitting limits on customers or sales. Inventory mistakes that can <a href=\"https://www.debtroundup.com/my-10000-excel-mistake/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">cost you $10,000</a> aren’t a problem, either.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>That flexibility carries over to the format, too<strong>.</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>You can go the guide route and create a downloadable how-to guide that walks people through your process, just like Robert Joyner does.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>He sells his <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.painthog.com/composition-design-for-the-expressive-artist\" target=\"_blank\">Painters Guide to Design &#38; Composition</a> for $79 a pop. </p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/art-design-and-composition.png?resize=800%2C263&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-26804\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/art-design-and-composition.png?resize=800%2C263&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/art-design-and-composition.png?resize=768%2C252&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/art-design-and-composition.png?resize=1536%2C504&#38;ssl=1 1536w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/art-design-and-composition.png?resize=2048%2C672&#38;ssl=1 2048w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Robert Joyner&#8217;s Complete Guide to Design and Composition</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Entrepreneur Marc Eglon takes it a step further and sells <a href=\"https://marc.podia.com/the-tiny-product-manual.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">The Tiny Product Manual</a> for $39, to help creators turn their lightbulb ideas into tiny products.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/33.png?resize=800%2C353&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Marc Eglon's Tiny Product Manual\" class=\"wp-image-25169\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/33.png?resize=800%2C353&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/33.png?resize=300%2C132&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/33.png?resize=150%2C66&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/33.png?resize=768%2C338&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/33.png?resize=990%2C436&#38;ssl=1 990w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/33.png?w=1071&#38;ssl=1 1071w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Marc Eglon&#8217;s Tiny Product Manual</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Another option is to make processes super simple and streamlined for people by offering plug-and-play templates. Designer entrepreneur Vanessa Ryan’s <a aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://vanessaryan.podia.com/boho-chic-toolbox\">Boho Chic Toolbox</a> sells a bundle of templates for designers for $225.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/34.png?resize=800%2C374&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Vanessa Ryan's Boho Chic Toolbox\" class=\"wp-image-25168\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/34.png?resize=800%2C374&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/34.png?resize=300%2C140&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/34.png?resize=150%2C70&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/34.png?resize=768%2C359&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/34.png?resize=990%2C462&#38;ssl=1 990w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/34.png?w=1060&#38;ssl=1 1060w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Vanessa Ryan&#8217;s Boho Chic Toolbox</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>OR you can go a little wild and create an off-the-beaten-path digital download like Chris Albon’s <a href=\"https://store.chrisalbon.com/machine-learning-flashcards\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">Machine Learning Flashcards</a>, which go for $12 for a package of 300.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/35.png?resize=800%2C372&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Chris Albon's Machine Learning Flashcards\" class=\"wp-image-25173\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/35.png?resize=800%2C372&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/35.png?resize=300%2C139&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/35.png?resize=150%2C70&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/35.png?resize=768%2C357&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/35.png?resize=990%2C460&#38;ssl=1 990w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/35.png?w=1044&#38;ssl=1 1044w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Chris Albon&#8217;s Machine Learning Flashcards</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Okay, you get the point.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Keep it relevant to your freelance copywriting business, of course, but there’s room to get creative with your format.</p>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">But as varied as digital download formats come, there’s one trait they all have in common (which you need to include):&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong><em>They make your target audience’s life easier.&#160;</em></strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">Put another way, jump on the ol&#8217; &#8220;offer value&#8221; bus and solve your audience’s problems.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>After all, you’ve written your blog to help people solve their problems in the first place, right?</p>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">Selling your digital download shouldn’t be any different.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Getting to the kind of income you can expect depends on your price. There are a few options for navigating pricing:&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.mbaskool.com/business-concepts/marketing-and-strategy-terms/6742-cost-based-pricing.html\" target=\"_blank\">Cost-based pricing</a> &#8211; Add your desired profit to the cost of producing your digital download</li><li><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.investopedia.com/terms/v/valuebasedpricing.asp\" target=\"_blank\">Value-based pricing</a> &#8211; Set your price at your audience’s perceived value</li><li><a href=\"https://www.accountingverse.com/managerial-accounting/pricing-decisions/competition-based-pricing.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">Competition-based pricing</a> &#8211; Use competitor pricing as a benchmark</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>Regardless of your pricing strategy, a good rule to follow is to price above your expenses, taxes <em>and</em> profits.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And not to be afraid of testing that price out.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Some businesses massively increase their revenue by testing their pricing. Take Server Density, for example, which tested two price points and converted fewer customers but increased their total revenue by a giant <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://vwo.com/success-stories/server-density/\" target=\"_blank\">114%</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/36.png?resize=800%2C229&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: How Server Density Used VWO to Increase Its Revenue by 114% \" class=\"wp-image-25174\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/36.png?resize=800%2C229&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/36.png?resize=300%2C86&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/36.png?resize=150%2C43&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/36.png?resize=768%2C220&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/36.png?w=841&#38;ssl=1 841w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: How Server Density Used VWO to Increase Its Revenue by 114% </figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Okay, that’s all gravy for a SaaS company like Server Density, but it’s not for everyone.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Be warned that testing your pricing strategy can also come with a <a href=\"https://www.priceintelligently.com/blog/bid/180676/why-you-should-never-a-b-test-your-pricing-strategy\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">couple of caveats</a>:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>It’s unlikely that your results will reach statistical significance (i.e., can’t be attributed to random chance)</li><li>You may price anchor and need to explain yourself (e.g., your no-longer-available lower price) to prospective customers</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>All in all: </strong>There’s no hard-fast rule to the type or price of digital download you sell. Get creative and offer something of value to your audience. See what they will &#8211; and won’t &#8211; pay for it.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If you do this well, you’ll scale your blog income. Our next monetizing tip also offers great scalability.</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>Sell an Online Course to Make Money Blogging</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Another lucrative way to monetize your blog is to package up your knowledge and sell it in the form of an online course. It’s a timely tactic, too.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Why? The market for elearning is on fire.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Its latest valuation was <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.gminsights.com/industry-analysis/elearning-market-size\" target=\"_blank\">$190 billion</a> just last year and is anticipated to grow beyond the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.gminsights.com/pressrelease/elearning-market\" target=\"_blank\">$300 billion</a> mark by 2025. And 40% of that market share is anticipated to come from North America, totaling <a href=\"https://elearningindustry.com/growth-of-the-elearning-market-gamut-size\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">$120 billion</a> by 2025.&#160; </p>\n\n\n\n<p>If you want to talk CAGR (compound annual growth rate), the elearning market is projected to grow at a <a href=\"https://www.gminsights.com/industry-analysis/elearning-market-size\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">7% CAGR</a> through the same time span.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/37.png?resize=530%2C315&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Global Market Insights - Industry Trends\" class=\"wp-image-25175\" width=\"530\" height=\"315\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/37.png?w=530&#38;ssl=1 530w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/37.png?resize=300%2C178&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/37.png?resize=150%2C89&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 530px) 100vw, 530px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Global Market Insights &#8211; Industry Trends</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>As far as what to focus your course on, choose a topic that combines your passion with your copywriting expertise <em>and </em>has profit potential.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>More specifically, list out a bunch of ideas and start plotting them on this Passion/Profit Matrix.<br></p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/38.png?resize=800%2C600&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-25176\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/38.png?resize=800%2C600&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/38.png?resize=300%2C225&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/38.png?resize=150%2C113&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/38.png?resize=768%2C576&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/38.png?resize=74%2C55&#38;ssl=1 74w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/38.png?resize=111%2C83&#38;ssl=1 111w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/38.png?resize=215%2C161&#38;ssl=1 215w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/38.png?resize=990%2C743&#38;ssl=1 990w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/38.png?w=1080&#38;ssl=1 1080w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>(Want a printer-friendly version of this matrix? Then check out this 12,000-word guide on <a href=\"https://www.podia.com/how-to-create-sell-profitable-online-course\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">how to create, sell and profit from online courses</a>.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>After you’re done plotting, choose the one from the upper-right quadrant that lights you up the most.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>This process is how Amanda Boleyn came up with <a href=\"https://www.shediditherwayshop.com/the-basics-of-building-a-business\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">The Basics of Building a Business</a> online course.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/39.png?resize=800%2C371&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Amanda Boleyn's The Basics of Building a Business Course\" class=\"wp-image-25177\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/39.png?resize=800%2C371&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/39.png?resize=300%2C139&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/39.png?resize=150%2C70&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/39.png?resize=768%2C356&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/39.png?resize=990%2C459&#38;ssl=1 990w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/39.png?w=1095&#38;ssl=1 1095w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Amanda Boleyn&#8217;s The Basics of Building a Business Course</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Although that’s not to say choosing your course topic should end there. There’s a pretty big next step you can’t ignore.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Validate and then validate again. (Makes it a two-part step, doesn’t it?)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>In other words, check in with your audience and find out if your course topic is something they want to learn about and are willing to pay for.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>To get useful feedback from your audience, reach out to them and ask questions. There are several ways to do this, so no excuses here:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Post about it on your social channels</li><li>DM people</li><li>Email your subscriber list</li><li>Run a poll or survey</li><li>Make phone calls</li><li>Chat with people face-to-face</li><li>Scour forums and groups and engage in conversations</li><li>Check out Amazon’s book inventory on the topic and read reviews</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>HOWEVER, it’s not enough just to ask. You need to <a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2018/05/how-to-listen/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">listen to what your customers want</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong><em>That’s </em></strong><strong>the key ingredient </strong>for complete market research validation. Once you do that, and only once you do that, you’ll find the effort worthwhile.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>How worthwhile? Exceedingly.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>That’s what entrepreneur Ryan Kulp’s experience was, anyway. Ryan <a href=\"https://twitter.com/ryanckulp/status/1146776396666155008\">tweeted to his audience</a> to validate his online course idea and <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.ryanckulp.com/niche-course-launch/\" target=\"_blank\">sold over $20,000</a> in online courses straight out of the gate.<br></p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/40.png?resize=539%2C499&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Ryan Kulp validated his course idea with a tweet\" class=\"wp-image-25178\" width=\"539\" height=\"499\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/40.png?w=539&#38;ssl=1 539w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/40.png?resize=300%2C278&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/40.png?resize=150%2C139&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 539px) 100vw, 539px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Ryan Kulp validated his course idea with a tweet</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Vincent Retg, a French entrepreneur who founded Le Musicien Formations, earned nearly 2,000 euros in online course sales in his first month offering his <a href=\"https://lemusicien.podia.com/melody-maker\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">Melody Maker</a> course.</p>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">Do you think he got there without validating his idea? (Spoiler: No, he definitely didn’t.)</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/41.png?resize=800%2C356&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Vincent Retg's Melody Maker course\" class=\"wp-image-25179\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/41.png?resize=800%2C356&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/41.png?resize=300%2C133&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/41.png?resize=150%2C67&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/41.png?resize=768%2C341&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/41.png?resize=990%2C440&#38;ssl=1 990w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/41.png?w=1165&#38;ssl=1 1165w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Vincent Retg&#8217;s Melody Maker course</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Finally, our beloved Michelle Gardner earned <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.debtroundup.com/my-10000-excel-mistake/\" target=\"_blank\">upwards of $434,698</a> selling a single online course.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/42.jpeg?resize=735%2C446&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Michelle Gardner earned $434,698+ from a single course\" class=\"wp-image-25180\" width=\"735\" height=\"446\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/42.jpeg?w=735&#38;ssl=1 735w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/42.jpeg?resize=300%2C182&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/42.jpeg?resize=150%2C91&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 735px) 100vw, 735px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Michelle Gardner earned $434,698+ from a single course</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Success with online courses is like a wheel. The more speed you pick up in one rotation, the faster the next one is…</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Every successful course launch puts you closer to <a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2017/09/course-launch-tech-stack/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">launching six-figure courses</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>How?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Going from blogger to online course seller is especially profitable as you gain traction and move further along in your blogging career. For pro bloggers who make over $25,000 in monthly income, a ginormous <a href=\"https://brandongaille.com/blog-income-report-study/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">80% of their income</a> is generated from online courses.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/43.png?resize=637%2C377&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: 2018 Blog Income Report Research Study - The Blog Millionaire\" class=\"wp-image-25181\" width=\"637\" height=\"377\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/43.png?w=637&#38;ssl=1 637w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/43.png?resize=300%2C178&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/43.png?resize=150%2C89&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 637px) 100vw, 637px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: 2018 Blog Income Report Research Study &#8211; The Blog Millionaire</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>However, while online courses are a burgeoning option for writers to monetize their blog, they’re far from the only solution.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If you don’t have the time and energy (or desire, for that matter) to create and market an online course &#8211; or if you&#8217;re not in a position to teach an entire course because, say, you&#8217;re not yet an expert on something &#8211; an ebook is another great info product to turn your fans into your patrons.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>Make Money by Selling Ebooks </h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Copyhackers started with four little ebooks, which brought in about $20K in 5 days and gave Jo the signal she needed to keep going with this biz. Today Copyhackers is a multi seven-figure business that <a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/thanks-here-is-your-ebook\">gives ebooks away</a> instead of selling &#8217;em &#8211; but it all started with those four ebooks. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Just like the elearning market, ebookers also enjoys a healthy CAGR. The global ebook market is expected to grow at a <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.statista.com/outlook/213/100/ebooks/worldwide#market-revenue\" target=\"_blank\">3.3% CAGR</a> through 2023. Its current valuation is nearly <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.statista.com/outlook/213/100/ebooks/worldwide#market-revenue\" target=\"_blank\">$13.7 billion in revenue</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/44.png?resize=800%2C413&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Statista\" class=\"wp-image-25182\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/44.png?resize=800%2C413&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/44.png?resize=300%2C155&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/44.png?resize=150%2C78&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/44.png?resize=768%2C397&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/44.png?w=807&#38;ssl=1 807w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Statista</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>The global breakdown is where things get really interesting for the ebook market. The countries with high Internet penetration are the zones with the greatest market share. Check it out by region.<br></p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/45.png?resize=561%2C334&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Statista\" class=\"wp-image-25183\" width=\"561\" height=\"334\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/45.png?w=561&#38;ssl=1 561w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/45.png?resize=300%2C179&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/45.png?resize=150%2C89&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/45.png?resize=559%2C334&#38;ssl=1 559w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 561px) 100vw, 561px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Statista</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>What does that mean for the near future? Look out for the quickly expanding Asia-Pacific region that’s welcoming digitalization and smart device penetration with open arms.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If you’re looking for topic ideas, go with a topic in your expertise wheelhouse that aligns with your passions <em>and </em>your business goals. Creating it will be more fun that way.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>(And trust me, you’re going to need a little fun in there. All hard work and no play makes Jack a frustrated freelancer.)</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>A few fun ebook examples&#8230;</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Spin up something like the creators of Pasta-based, Matt and Steph, did with their <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://shop.pastabased.com/vegan-italian-thanksgiving-ebook\" target=\"_blank\">Complete Vegan Italian Thanksgiving</a> ebook.</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/46.png?resize=800%2C377&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Creators of Pasta-based Matt and Steph's Complete Vegan Italian Thanksgiving ebook\" class=\"wp-image-25184\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/46.png?resize=800%2C377&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/46.png?resize=300%2C141&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/46.png?resize=150%2C71&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/46.png?resize=768%2C362&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/46.png?w=975&#38;ssl=1 975w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Creators of Pasta-based Matt and Steph&#8217;s Complete Vegan Italian Thanksgiving ebook</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>Or something similar to what entrepreneur, David Delahunty, created with his 5 Ideas a Day ebook (page no longer exists).</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/47.png?resize=800%2C327&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"David Delahunty's 5 Ideas a Day Ebook\" class=\"wp-image-25185\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/47.png?resize=800%2C327&#38;ssl=1 800w, 990w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/47.png?w=1155&#38;ssl=1 1155w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>David Delahunty&#8217;s 5 Ideas a Day Ebook</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>As for anticipated earnings, selling an ebook can potentially put you over the edge and earn enough money to quit your full-time gig.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>That’s what it did for creator Justin Jackson. In 2016, he was able to take the plunge from blogging side-hustler to full-time entrepreneur thanks to his ebook <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://devmarketing.xyz/\" target=\"_blank\">Marketing for Developers</a>.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>In fact, selling his ebook was the final ingredient needed to bring in <a href=\"https://www.podia.com/articles/how-justin-jackson-made-over-100-000-on-podia\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">$146,000 in revenue</a> that year.&#160;&#160;&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And Justin did so well with his ebook that he created an online course version of it. (Can you say gravy on top of gravy? His ebook practically became income poutine.)</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/48.png?resize=800%2C626&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Justin Jackson's Marketing for Developers Ebook and Course\" class=\"wp-image-25186\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/48.png?resize=800%2C626&#38;ssl=1 800w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/48.png?resize=300%2C235&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/48.png?resize=150%2C117&#38;ssl=1 150w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/48.png?resize=768%2C601&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/48.png?w=935&#38;ssl=1 935w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Justin Jackson&#8217;s Marketing for Developers Ebook and Course</figcaption></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>If you decide to go the ebook route, though, it comes with a caveat.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Sure, the global market size projections look great, BUT there’s contending evidence that points to both ebook sales dropping <em>and </em>ebook sales growing.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Whaa?&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>A quick explanation:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>In 2017, there was a contentious announcement that <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://www.publishersweekly.com/pw/by-topic/digital/content-and-e-books/article/76706-e-book-sales-fell-10-in-2017.html\" target=\"_blank\">ebook sales fell 10%</a>, which meant that 450 represented publishers witnessed a drop in ebook sales from <a href=\"https://www.geekwire.com/2018/traditional-publishers-ebook-sales-drop-indie-authors-amazon-take-off/\">180 million to 162 million units</a> within a year.</p>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">While that may appear to be a bleak outlook, there’s actually growth in the nitty-gritty detail. Reporting on that same year, Amazon’s Jeff Bezos <a href=\"https://twitter.com/amazonnews/status/998666743760515072\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">announced</a> that “over 1,000 independent authors surpassed $100,000 in royalties in 2017 through Kindle Direct Publishing.”</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/49.png?resize=526%2C409&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Amazon News tweet\" class=\"wp-image-25187\" width=\"526\" height=\"409\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/49.png?w=526&#38;ssl=1 526w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/49.png?resize=300%2C233&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/49.png?resize=150%2C117&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 526px) 100vw, 526px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>Amazon News tweet</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Which means: </strong>Traditional publisher ebook sales declined while indie-published ebooks soared.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And to further confuse the market stats, popular Data Guy’s proclamation that <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://the-digital-reader.com/2018/10/25/data-guy-unmasked-on-linkedin-as-bookstat-ceo-paul-abbassi/\" target=\"_blank\">ebook sales doubled in 2018</a> in the U.S. was refuted by <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://thenewpublishingstandard.com/ebook-sales-doubled-us-2018-according-data-guys-nonsensical-bookstat-numbers/\" target=\"_blank\">The New Publish Standard’s article</a> that stated, “the industry data we’ve seen so far… paints a highly misleading picture of the market.”</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/50.png?resize=508%2C198&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: The New Publish Standard\" class=\"wp-image-25188\" width=\"508\" height=\"198\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/50.png?w=508&#38;ssl=1 508w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/50.png?resize=300%2C117&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/50.png?resize=150%2C58&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 508px) 100vw, 508px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: The New Publish Standard</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>How’s that for a dichotomy?</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>The main takeaway (and our recommended solution to selling your ebook) is to self-publish your ebook</strong> and either:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Sell it through your own site if you want all the profits or&#160;</li><li>Sell it through Amazon with one hand in your pocket poised to hand back some of your revenue.&#160;</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<h3>10 steps to self-publish an ebook</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Jo&#8217;s going to create a program on writing and self-publishing an ebook as part of Copyhackers&#8217;s upcoming Content School. But for now, to self-publish your ebook, we recommend these 10 simple steps:</p>\n\n\n\n<ol><li>Decide on your ebook topic</li><li>Record yourself talking about your topic</li><li>Get your recording transcribed</li><li>Sit down (or stand!) and turn your transcript into a great draft</li><li>Title it</li><li>Proofread it, format it and add your images</li><li>Design your ebook cover</li><li>Convert it to a digital download file </li><li>Price your ebook</li><li>Publish your ebook to your storefront and sell</li></ol>\n\n\n\n<p>Pretty straightforward, right?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Phew &#8211; that’s five of the best routes to monetize a blog. Let’s recap.</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Do you need to carve out an ad budget to make money blogging?</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>One word: Nope.</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Do you need to hit all five of these best blog monetization methods to restock your bank account?</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Three words: Most certainly, no.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Even if you only carry out <em>one</em>, you’ll be miles ahead of zero blog income. It doesn’t even really matter which one it is, either.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>A whopping<a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"http://www.techclient.com/blogging-statistics/\" target=\"_blank\"> 61% of consumers</a> make a purchase based on a blog post they’ve read, which means at least 61% of your readers are primed for monetization.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/51.png?resize=636%2C163&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Tech Client - Blogging Statistics\" class=\"wp-image-25189\" width=\"636\" height=\"163\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/51.png?w=636&#38;ssl=1 636w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/51.png?resize=300%2C77&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/51.png?resize=150%2C38&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 636px) 100vw, 636px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Tech Client &#8211; Blogging Statistics</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>In other words, if you have <em>anything useful at all </em>to sell to your audience, chances are your blog-reading audience will buy it. (After all, you’re their trusted source who authors the content they’ve been eating up).&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>HOWEVER, the more blog monetization channels you tap into, the better off you’ll be.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\"><strong>Translation: </strong>Diversify your blog income (i.e., try as many of these five blog monetization tactics as you can) to earn more money. The more you diversify, the more you’ll earn.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>For the cherry on top, let’s go back to our iconic blog monetization king, John Lee Dumas, one more time.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">In September, 2019, his revenue from sponsorships and affiliate revenue are basically even stevens.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/52.png?resize=610%2C379&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Entrepreneurs on Fire \" class=\"wp-image-25190\" width=\"610\" height=\"379\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/52.png?w=610&#38;ssl=1 610w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/52.png?resize=300%2C186&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/52.png?resize=150%2C93&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 610px) 100vw, 610px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Entrepreneurs on Fire </figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>But that wasn’t the case <em>just six months ago</em>. Affiliate revenue accounted for almost half of his blog income then.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/52.png?resize=610%2C379&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"From: Entrepreneurs on Fire\" class=\"wp-image-25190\" width=\"610\" height=\"379\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/52.png?w=610&#38;ssl=1 610w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/52.png?resize=300%2C186&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/52.png?resize=150%2C93&#38;ssl=1 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 610px) 100vw, 610px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /><figcaption>From: Entrepreneurs on Fire </figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p class=\"has-text-align-left\">Imagine how much more that change would’ve hurt if he had less streams to rely on. Or, at the very least, imagine how much more <em>stagnant </em>his income would be if he didn’t keep it varied.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Now, be like John, ditch the ads and start loading up your plate with the buffet spread of blog monetization tactics:&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Secure sponsors for your blog posts and review products and services of like-minded businesses</li><li>Include affiliate links in your blog and receive a commission each time someone purchases</li><li>Create a digital download and sell it on your blog</li><li>Productize your knowledge with an online course and sell it to your blog readers</li><li>Self-publish an ebook and sell it to your blog audience</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>It’s a choose-your-own-adventure kind of party, so long as you do actually choose. 8-664_d77c09a3ef07971e.webp","https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/22.png?resize=789%2C429&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn89@2020_4/2020/08/25/02-39-09-649_2a297a6c106c8a46.webp","https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/23.png?resize=800%2C620&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn10@2020_6/2020/08/25/02-39-05-285_93d26593e9b6893c.webp","https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/24.png?resize=800%2C373&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn77@2020_6/2020/08/25/02-39-01-005_c1047ca8234d8648.webp","https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/25.png?resize=800%2C527&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn21@2020_1/2020/08/25/02-39-03-617_72c297a03724b2af.webp","https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/26.jpg?resize=628%2C278&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn61@2020_6/2020/08/25/02-39-03-283_d13090def289b85f.webp","https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/27.png?resize=800%2C352&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn89@2020_3/2020/08/25/02-39-01-070_d7ab7a525760c239.webp","https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/28.png?resize=689%2C428&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn86@2020_4/2020/08/25/02-39-02-248_40799ac2a5af6de0.webp","https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/29.png?resize=560%2C465&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn85@2020_5/2020/08/25/02-39-05-228_0942d397a3b9560c.webp","https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/30.png?resize=800%2C357&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn21@2020_4/2020/08/25/02-39-02-042_300b81396c1a146c.webp","https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/31.png?ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn25@2020_4/2020/08/25/02-39-04-668_1a173efdf2e4a526.webp","https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/upload :"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn37@2020_3/2020/08/25/02-39-08-394_df85018b7e346592.webp","https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/43.png?resize=637%2C377&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn18@2020_2/2020/08/25/02-39-01-030_9ed48762f91a2a22.webp","https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/44.png?resize=800%2C413&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn62@2020_6/2020/08/25/02-39-08-498_30ad7fff99abc685.webp","https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/45.png?resize=561%2C334&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn50@2020_3/2020/08/25/02-39-01-043_064a3994fa15373f.webp","https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/46.png?resize=800%2C377&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn42@2020_2/2020/08/25/02-39-09-233_ff566b3a12762841.webp","https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/47.png?resize=800%2C327&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn82@2020_2/2020/08/25/02-39-02-283_e49e2eb2041c5738.webp","https://i2.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/48.png?resize=800%2C626&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn42@2020_2/2020/08/25/02-39-03-075_f892ad11fb3cf0b9.webp","https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/49.png?resize=526%2C409&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn69@2020_3/2020/08/25/02-39-08-573_819b692a8beda05c.webp","https://i0.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/50.png?resize=508%2C198&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn1@2020_1/2020/08/25/02-39-09-059_cb61f63dc559e954.webp","https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/51.png?resize=636%2C163&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn49@2020_4/2020/08/25/02-39-04-005_5aedd793c1b10eb2.webp","https://i1.wp.com/copyhackers.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/52.png?resize=610%2C379&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn21@2020_1/2020/08/25/02-39-02-881_dea5ba0609422445.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598323135052},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 10:38:55","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 10:38:55","title":"What Is a Swipe File? And Why Does Every Copywriter Need One?","link":"https://copyhackers.com/?p=24651","description":"\n<p><em>A swipe file is a collection of memorable content you can use for copywriting ideas. Save emails, pages, ads, etc. in your &#8220;swipe file.&#8221; And refer to your swipes for inspiration (and in place of templates) when you start writing.</em></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Do you look at the blank screen and feel unprepared to write copy?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Then you should add an organized swipe file to your copywriting toolbox. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>I depend on my swipe file for the many copywriting projects I work on as a conversion copywriter at Copyhackers Agency. </p>\n\n\n\n<h2>This is how I set up my swipe file</h2>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>I save screenshots of pages and ads in swipe folders within Google Drive, which I share with our team</li><li>I star emails in Gmail, which sends them to <a href=\"http://airstory.co\">Airstory</a> as cards I can reference later, when I&#8217;m writing in Airstory</li><li>I also have a bunch of swipe-file folders set up in Gmail, and I move different emails to those folders</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>If you&#8217;re starting out with an email swipe file, consider using these folder names in Gmail, to organize the emails you&#8217;ll be saving:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Email Swipes: Welcome emails</li><li>Email Swipes: Nurturing emails</li><li>Email Swipes: Sales emails</li><li>Email Swipes: Cart abandonment emails</li><li>Email Swipes: Upsells and cross-sells</li><li>Email Swipes: SDR / 1-to-1 </li><li>Email Swipes: Other</li><li>Email Swipes: DIFFERENT</li><li>Email Swipes: BEST</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>What goes under &#8220;Different&#8221; and &#8220;Best&#8221;?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>That&#8217;s where you&#8217;ll save emails that are, respectively, different from the norm or expectations &#8211; which may or may not be good &#8211; and extremely, extremely awesome. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Keep in mind: A swipe file is a collection of ads and content you like. You probably have no idea if it&#8217;s performing well. So use your swipe file as inspiration &#8211; not as a Bible. </p>\n\n\n\n<h2>Here is an example of a swipe file </h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Let’s say you need to write a homepage for a client in the fitness industry. Even with research in hand, you could use a little inspiration to get started. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>A collection of fitness-specific landing pages, like this, would help you:</p>\n\n\n\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/H7tGl2G06XZUMRsQcQSEHd6yIST5AdDda7yfuM9k72UZOBeY1LUfC4q0HZ5AOrvaTPkOB1jH6l9Ex2cNAOh8ghJnUiC3afPXvo5DmkjiTLiIqDAJVO3knTlLrvjqxQwgbgdO3y-i\" alt=\"Example of a swipe file of fitness home pages\"/></figure>\n\n\n\n<p>This is not the time to <em>start</em> looking for pages to swipe because I guarantee you will not find what you’re looking for. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>You will, in fact, end up spending the next few hours sliding deeper and deeper into your search only to find yourself holding a serious opinion about the merits of a didgeridoo performance on Australia’s Got Talent.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2>How to start swiping&#160;</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Get yourself in the habit of collecting swipes regularly. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>For example, start with websites and swipe the following pages (by taking screenshots of them):</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>Home&#160;</li><li>Pricing&#160;</li><li>Features&#160;</li><li>Demo&#160;</li><li>About</li><li>Blog</li><li>Resources</li><li>Customer success</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>Then you can further categorize your swipe files by industry. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>You don’t have to start with websites, of course. You can start with landing pages, or thank you pages or opt-in pop-ups. It doesn’t matter. What matters is getting in the habit of taking screenshots and adding them to your swipe file.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Let me repeat that it’s the <a href=\"https://www.sciencedaily.com/releases/2014/08/140808111931.htm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">habit</a> part that’s important here. Make it a part of your routine. Set reminders for yourself. The more you remember to do it, the easier it will become.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2>Swipe files are filled with work that may outperform the control or may not (you have no idea, usually)</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>When you consult your swipes, you likely won’t know whether or not it converted well &#8211; unless you’re adding swipes like <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2016/06/great-home-page-copy/\" target=\"_blank\">this home page copy that beat the control</a> or <a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2017/08/saas-onboarding-email/\">thiS SaaS onboarding sequence that beat the control</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The point is not to copy the swipe word for word, obviously. The purpose is guidance and learning:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>How an argument is presented</li><li>How pricing levels are compared</li><li>How offers are positioned</li><li>What the tone and voice were</li><li>Etc.</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>It’s meant to help you find a starting point or give you ideas about what else you may want to include that bolsters the case you’re making with your copy.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Even if you know an email performed well &#8211; and you use it for inspiration &#8211; it doesn’t guarantee the email <em>you write</em> will perform well.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Using swipes should be just one part of your overall copywriting process. A process that should also include <a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/a-super-speedy-formula-to-find-voc-fast/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"research (opens in a new tab)\">research</a> into the product or service, the audience and competitors.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<h2>What details should you record in your swipe file?</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>So what should you be looking for in your swipes? &#8211; beyond types of pages, industries and categories?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>If you want to dig a little deeper into what’s going on behind the copy (and I hope you do), then you could look for any of the following:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><strong>A big idea:</strong> Is there one? How is it threaded through the page or email campaign?</li><li><strong>Messaging hierarchy:</strong> Can you follow a conversation? Or is it muddled?</li><li><strong>Formula or frameworks: </strong>Is there one? Is it used well?</li><li><strong>Voice of customer:</strong> Does it sound like something a customer would say? Or the way a marketer would talk?</li><li><strong>Emotion:</strong> What emotion or outcome is being sold? Where is the emotion used?</li><li><strong>Elements of persuasion:</strong> Is there social proof provided? Are testimonials supporting the conversion?</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>This is not a comprehensive list. If you’re a veteran copywriter, then you know there’s a long list of <a href=\"https://copyhackers.com/2015/10/copywriting-formula/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">copywriting formulas and techniques</a> you can look for and categorize.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And if you’re new to copywriting, I’d suggest you supplement your swipe file by reading <a href=\"https://www.amazon.ca/Adweek-Copywriting-Handbook-Advertising-Copywriters/dp/0470051248/ref=asc_df_0470051248/?tag=googleshopc0c-20&#38;linkCode=df0&#38;hvadid=292914274695&#38;hvpos=1o1&#38;hvnetw=g&#38;hvrand=11554012652743189212&#38;hvpone=&#38;hvptwo=&#38;hvqmt=&#38;hvdev=c&#38;hvdvcmdl=&#38;hvlocint=&#38;hvlocphy=9001494&#38;hvtargid=pla-450155118208&#38;psc=1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\">books about copywriting</a>, or blogs about copywriting like Copyhackers (<a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" aria-label=\"here's a good place to start (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://copyhackers.com/3-part-conversion-copywriting-process-for-newbies/\" target=\"_blank\">here&#8217;s a good place for newbies to start</a>). Many resources will include samples of well-performing ads and sales pages you can learn from.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>By collecting swipes, you’re filling your copywriting toolbox with inspiration and ideas that help you get started on a project. Because there’s not much that’s worse than staring at a blank screen and not knowing what to do first.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>With a swipe file you can try out a few ideas and see what works best &#8211; it may take a few tries, but it’s still better than paralysis and anxiety.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Once you see how much a swipe file can help with your writing process, you’ll never want to write without one.</p>\n<script type=\"text/javascript\">\n\nwindow.rmpanda = window.rmpanda || {};\nwindow.rmpanda.wpvars = window.rmpanda.wpvars || {};\n\nvar debug = (window.rmpanda || {}).debug || /rmdebug=1/.test(window.location.search);\nvar logger = {};\nObject.keys(console).forEach(f => {\n\tif (typeof console[f] === 'function') {\n\t\tlogger[f] = function() {\n\t\t\tdebug && console[f].apply(console, Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments));\n\t\t};\n\t}\n});\n\nfunction pipelistToArray(pipelist) {\n\treturn (pipelist || '').replace(/^\\||\\|$/g, '').split('|');\n}\n\nfunction arrayToPipelist(array) {\n\treturn '|' + (array || []).join('|') + '|';\n}\n\nfunction createLeaderboard(cachedPosts, dataKey) {\n\tvar leaderboard = {};\n\tvar totalRead = cachedPosts.length;\n\n\tcachedPosts.forEach(function(pageview, idx) {\n\t\tvar pID = pageview[0];
